***запасть.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:запасть.html>запа́сть</a> (15036)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">за-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">za-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:пасть.html>пасть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">pastʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:запасть.html>запа́сть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">zapástʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> (<i>imperfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:западать.html>запада́ть</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to fall back, to fall behind, to sink down</li>
<li>to sink deeply
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:слово.html>слова́</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:он.html>его́</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:запасть.html>запа́ли</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:он.html>мне</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:в.html>в</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:душа.html>ду́шу</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">slová jevó <b>zapáli</b> mne v dúšu</i> ― <span class="e-translation">his words imprinted themselves in my mind [on my soul]; his words sank home</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">slang</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to take <i>(to)</i>, to fall <i>(for)</i></li></ol>

<ul><li><span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:запад.html>за́пад</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">západ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></li></ul>

***запах.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:запах.html>запах</a> (785)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_1">Etymology 1</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:запах.html>за́пах</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">zápax</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:запах.html>за́паха</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:запах.html>за́пахи</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:запах.html>за́пахов</a></b>)
</p>

<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">за-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">za-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:переть.html>пере́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">perétʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:запереть.html>запере́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">zaperétʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> (<i>imperfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:запирать.html>запира́ть</a></b>)

<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:запечатлеть.html>запечатле́ть</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:поцеловать.html>поцелу́й</a> (<a href = vnd.unilang:на.html>на</a>)</i> <span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">literary<span class="ib-comma qualifier-comma">,</span> dated</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>zapečatlétʹ</b> pocelúj (na)</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to imprint a kiss (on)</span></div></dd></dl></li>

<p><b><a href = vnd.unilang:запивать.html>запива́вший</a></b>
</p><p><a href = vnd.unilang:действительный.html>Действи́тельное</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:причастие.html>прича́стие</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:прошедший.html>проше́дшего</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:время.html>вре́мени</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:тип.html>тип</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:склонение.html>склоне́ния</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:классификация.html>классифика́ции</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:а.html>А</a>. Зализняка — 4a.

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:запивать.html>запива́ть</a> (10967)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:запить.html>запи́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">zapítʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ва́ть</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-vátʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:запивать.html>запива́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">zapivátʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:запить.html>запи́ть</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to wash down <i>(with)</i>, to take <i>(after/with)</i>
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:запивать.html>запива́ть</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:лекарство.html>лека́рство</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:молоко.html>молоко́м</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>zapivátʹ</b> lekárstvo molokóm</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to take milk with one's medicine</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>to take to drink, to go on a drinking bout/spree</li></ol>

***запинаться.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:запинаться.html>запина́ться</a> (15482)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">за-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">za-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:пинать.html>пина́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">pinátʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ся</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-sja</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:запинаться.html>запина́ться</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">zapinátʹsja</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:запнуться.html>запну́ться</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to stumble, to halt
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:запинаться.html>запина́ться</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:о.html>о</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:камень.html>ка́мень</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>zapinátʹsja</b> o kámenʹ</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to stumble on/against a stone</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>to stammer, to falter, to stop short</li></ol>
